---
title:      MARC21 structure in JSON
layout:     post
date:       2018-01-28 00:00:00
author:     "pkiraly"
customjs:
 - http://code.jquery.com/jquery-1.4.2.min.js
 - http://pkiraly.github.io/js/table.js
---

This page displayes MARC21 structure in formatted JSON format. It is generated from the Java classes which describe the structure. There are some more attributes which is not exported into the JSON format, but it is a work in progress. If you miss something, please let me know via the [issue tracker](https://github.com/pkiraly/metadata-qa-marc/issues/45). Credits: the JSON schema was requested by [Jakob Vo√ü](https://twitter.com/nichtich) and [Johann Rolschewski](https://twitter.com/johrols/).

A raw version is avalable [here](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/pkiraly/metadata-qa-marc/master/src/main/resources/marc-schema.json).

<!-- more -->

To generate the file from the [program](https://github.com/pkiraly/metadata-qa-marc/):

```bash
./common-script
java -cp $JAR de.gwdg.metadataqa.marc.cli.MappingToJson > marc-schema.json
```
or
```bash
java -cp target/metadata-qa-marc-0.2-SNAPSHOT-jar-with-dependencies.jar de.gwdg.metadataqa.marc.cli.MappingToJson > marc-schema.json
```
(The version name will be changed in the future)


```JavaScript
{
```
